ryght excellent kynge aboue al redoubted▪ assemble hoost men warre haste yt maye sende vnto cyte lyon comen yssued almayne moo hondreth thousande fyghtyngemen wyll dystroy realme put subgeceyon whan kynge pepyn vnderstonden tydynges much basshed made come hym archebysshop reyns duke myllon dangler▪ geruais sampson tolde wordes messenger demaunded counsayll yf sholde go towarde acquytaine socoure good duke sauary▪ towarde lyon defende coūtre ye whiche thynge answered myllon dangler syr vpō mater must counsaylled shyrte nerer body gowne yo • oughte defende countree another lette owne byleueth coū sayll accepted it▪ sayd vnto ye messenger good duke sauary tyme myght socoure mayster behoued hym lede hoost toward lyon tell lorde kepe hym wel tyll haue done shal coure hym wt grete retorned acquytayne tolde tydynges lettyng kynge pepyn whan duke sauary vnderstode might haue socoure ye kynge pepyn moche sorowful ye grene knyght made hym grete warre assyeged hym nere ought knowe grene knyghte broder vnto ferragus gyaunt kepte lady bellyssant castell whiche ualentines moder wylde orsons haue herde declared ¶ ye duke sauary within acquitayne right pensyf sorowfull ye grene knyghte made hym suche warre doughter made cryed commaunded hoost sholde harneys vnto suche case apperteyned morowe mornynge wolde yssue vpō ye grene knyght fyght euery body put himselfe poynt dyde theyr dylygence arme whan daye clere trompettes clarons dyde wne men armes euery syde well horsbacke fote put hem vpon waye yssue oute cyte grete haste duke sauary assayll grene knyght suche weneth auaunce hymself oftentymes owne dōmage happened vnto duke shal duke sauary yssued acquytaine great company whan vpon feld made sown trompettes clarons valyaunt champyon assayll enemyes smote amongest theym sarazyns painims grete nombre rynne vnto armes began meruayllous fyerse batayll grene knyght sinote wyth axe armes myghtye stroke fyrste entre slewe two knyghtes duke sauary drewe ward hym assaylled ech ryght fiersely good duke much valyaunt that▪ grete foly enterprised fight grene knyght predestynacyon hym suche shuld neuer conquered vamquysshed man shoulde kynges sonne neuer bene nourysshed womanne souked theyr brestes thought suche man myght neuer founden child vpon earth shal fyght wyth hym vaynquyssh hym orson sauage shal afterwarde duke sauary grene knight fought longe togyder good duke sauary entred ferre whan wend haue withdrawn hoste enclosed wyth painyms sarazyns toke hym prysoner led hym vnto grene knighte whiche ryght gladde hym wolde haue let go treasure good duke sauery reclaymed god virgin marye hys herte whan chrystan men knew duke taken retorned acquitayne heuy sorowfull began people make greate dole sorowe cytie acquytayne wepynge bytterlye theyr good duke loued muche thre sone garyn▪ anseline▪ garyn yō gest made grete dole theyr fader aboue al sorowe lamentacions fezonne passed teared shining golde wepte full bytterly pleasaunt eyen sayd ala euyl houre borne whan many noble knyghtes vassalles must suffre hydeous deathes pyteous lamentacyons yet thyng hert greueth • muche good duke father handes hys mortal ennemyes sake behoueth hym fynyshe dayes sorowe dystresse ala ryght dere fader muche haue loued whan loue sold derely must suffre death therfore thus complained fezonne full soore wepyng wil courage haue slayne self lady letted grene knyght hys pauyllyon made good duke brought sayde vnto hym ryght fyersly seest thou thou art subgeccyon tyme haue puysaunce saue spyll shall tell thou shalte gyue thy doughter fezonne vnto wife thys doynge thy lyfe shal saued shal leade thy greane mountayne shal make rychely crowned sarazin said duke shal tel wyl know thou shalt neuer haue doughter thou make baptyzed byleue jhesu christ sauary sayd greane knighte neuer speke vnto suche thynge neuer dayes life wyl byleue thy god yet tel thou wil beleue counsall shal make dye fynysshe thy dayes vyllaynouslye yet tel shal make acquitaine brente putte execucyon menne womenne chyldren lytle great shall make suffer deathe paynym sayde duke sauary god inestimable grace kepe thy furour great cruelnesse hym trust hym onely conforte longe speakyng mater bothe grene knyght duke sauary reclaymynge god syghed full tenderlye greane knyght beheld hym whan saw great lamentacyons hee made▪ pyteous teares hee wept sayd vnto free duke leue thy wepyng esprysed loue thy doughter ardauntly enbraced loue haue talent courage put vnto deth tally delibered let go vnder condiciō thou shalt finde knight wythin thys syxe monethes strength armes maye wyn thy doughter agaynst thou shall retorne home countre agayne wythal myne host wythout tynge destroyinge lande yf happen conquered ouer comen within ye sayd terame shal haue thy doughter vnto wyfe drynke brede water ye cursed sarazins grete staues theyr • ystes smote vppon two chyldren without hauynge ony pyte dogges dongeon full fylthe • r • ure caste lete downe whan pryson sette theyr knee cry • ge god mercy praynge wolde forgyue thē theyr synnes neuer wende haue comen oute place ferragus hadde thus enprysoned uale • tyne orson mounted vp palais made brought hym fayre clerymonde wepte pyteously ye teres yssued eyen face wepte syster said ferragus leue wepinge chaū ge courage mahowne god haue longe byleued ye hed brasse whan wyll wed take maryage straunger oute byleue whome haue herte varyable wyll woman whan wyll loue yt hathe shewed himselfe mortal enemye broder grene knyghte well appertayneth haue man worthy hygher lygnage yf wyl bileue wyll shall gyue husbā de puyssaunt kinge tromparte▪ whiche maye season hyghelyfe rychely honoured therfore forgete two chrysten frēshmen haue truste shal make dye hanged necke broder said clerymonde behoueth obeye vnto commaundement one muste • ere passe lyghtly thige maye haue force constrayneth ryght hath vertue necessyte maketh oftentymes man • ell good chene wordes fynysshed ferragus dyde departe quene wyfe entred hall whiche grete honoure reuerence hath receyued fayre clerimonde sayinge syster ryght welcome hether hadde ryght greate desyre se lady sayd clerimonde thancke hondred tymes knowe ryghte sorowful dyspleasaunt two christen knight whiche broder ferragus vnder vmbre surenes loyalte hathe made passe sea hathe put obscare prysone vyle abhomynable grete dispite hathe sworne dethe yf forsake theyr lawe byleue alasse dere syster true shoulde haue one knightes mariages among al liuing menne mooste fayrest mooste valyaunt moost hardy force armes hathe conquered loue wherfore lady beseche counsayl haue grete nede also shewe christen woman whych haue kepte longe castell fayre syster said quene may se spake bellyssant sayd ladye wil speke hardely haue grete desire speke ala lady bring tidings wyll make gladde sorowful dysplesaunt know certainte estate lyfe knowe veray treuth pebe sister vnto king pepin wyfe vnto emperour grece wronge againste righte hathe banysshed empyre soone deliuered two fayre sonnes forest wherof one taken away wild bere lost tell chyldren yet lyue knowe place whereas may fynde theym wordes quene bellyssant fel vnto earth swowne ioye pyte hadde clerymonde toke vp muche great chere trauayled sore went bedde slepte pacolet slepte ryght dylygent gere playe crafte came great towre whereof gate tyne stele great thycke surely locked also soone casten sorte gate opened locke broke entred vntyll came doore pryson thyldren also soone touched dore opeded brake gate dydde two chyldren darke pytharde dore open ioyned handes deuoutly kneled downe earth cryed god mercye wende well gyaunt ferragus hadde sent make dye ualentyne began wepe tenderly orson sayde hym take comforte pacience behoueth v die finishe day se clerely syth soo se none remedy thynke venge dye hym fortune perpllous aduentures ben al tyme theyr lyues vnto present houre ¶ whan ualentine finisshed wordes empresse bellissāt knewe clerely propre child naturall loue asperly taken greter haboundaunce acquitaine ca xxxvi also soone hadde taken londe wente vnto strongè castell ualentyne euer hadde feare ferragus soiourned longe retourned vnto port badde maryners stuffe theyr galee vytaylles artyllerye shold redy depart whan called vpon retorned vnto castel without makyng onye semblaūt sayd vnto hys moder bellissant lady clerimonde woulde goo grece towarde constantinoble se father themperoure alexander wyth wronge agaynst ryghte expulsed hys mother wylobeyed lady also orson pacolet mounted sea perfourme vyage daye cleare houre approched gayler kynge ferragus accustomed go se hys prysoners wente toward greate toure bare bread water gyue eate whan gate prysone open saw wel prysoners gone retorned hastely toward kynge ferragus sayde hym great feare syr aske mercy thys nyght haue lost two christen knyghtes prisoner gyuen kepe saying wordes aryued messenger sayd hye assistentes puyssaunt king ferragus greate mischefe hapned tonight place haue lost christen woman haue kepte heauy theym yssued oute gate without hors soo great heuy payne myght fynde ony hors woulde beare great head black hear styffe wylde hogges br • st • lles hys armes greate boned shoulder large legges acquytayne ¶ ualentyne orson vpon see haue herde entred cyte acquytayne▪ without makynge • ny mencyon estate vnto ony persone straunge men lodged burgeys ualentyne wolde haue gone gladly duke sauaryes palays orson aduysed hym grete subtylyte sayd vnto broder ualentyne maner wyse broder haue aduysed thynkynge selfe nature wyll woman varyable lightely chaūged cause delibered mencyon shall made comynge vnto tyme maye knowe euydente sygne fayre fezonne reclamed soo muche dere louer yf haue chaunged courage broder sayd valentyne shall well done yf shall subtylly wrought orson clothed habyte knyght sought auentures toke lytell pacolet squyer wente towarde palays entred halle duke acquytayne lycence gardes whan hym salued hym made hym reuerence suche appertayned vnto hym dó suche thinge wyse well lerned whan salued duke behelde hym moche well hym thought orson bycause spake knewe studyed sayd hym knyght tell bryngeth hether free duke sayd orson knyght aduenturous gladly wolde fide maner auenture good loyall seruyce body knyght sayd duke grete fayre thynketh sholde valyaūte hardy armes therfore yf wyll serue shall gyue suche wage shall contente may muche wyl pleasure departe shal make rychest kynne gramercy sayd orson shall deserue shall moche maye knowe laya • te poore puyssaunce knyght sayd duke reteyne courte grete trust haue seruyce hondred pounde parysii ye serue ony ferder shall make delyuer soo moche orson wyse well taught maners countenaunce prudence mayntene reteyned hym palays made hym dyne knyghtes whan ye table maners countenaunce soo pleasaunt agreable euery body baron knyghtes moche beholden aboue thynges ladyes damoy selles aduysed fayre fezonne sworne wyfe ye whiche grete melancolye grete beaute wolde neuer haue wenue ben orson habyte language maner dyned orson ye duke courte whan came dyner duke called tresorer made delyuered vnto hym hondred pounde parisu hadde promysed hym orson toke leue tyme thankynge noble largesse promy singe hym faith wolde serue hym truely necessyte retorned vnto lodgynge noble ladyes abode hym whan comen vnto tolde recountred vnto duke grete honoure hadde reteyned hym soudyoure wage wherat laughed moche made grete ioye happened weke duke acquytayne certaine fydinges y• kynge ferragus dyscended make hym warre sent subgectes baron knyghtes byddynge come socoure hym redy harneys abyde batayll yf nede syth made cyte vytaylled haboundauntly bothe flesshe whete defende countree kepe cyte acquytayne againste kynge ferragus whiche weke set syege acquytayne propre place broder grene knyght pyght pauylyon whā vaynquysshed orson orete large meruaylously siege paynyms sarazyas dyde ryght grete dommage countree acquytayne theyr arryuay▪ kepte countre greate subgec • yon domynacy thought wel ha ue conquered countree haue dystroyed christen men ye noble duke acquytayne moche hardy valyaunt made anone arme men grete notable company baron knyghtes yssued cyte acquytaine fyghte agaynste paynyms armes fyght agaynst kynge ferragus ¶ haw duke acquytayne taken batayll feragus orson delpuered hym ayde pacolet capitulo xxxviii whan good duke acquitayne sawe ye hoost sarazins moche grete large recōmaunded hym vnto god herte praynge hym defender day made ordeyne bataylles blowe trompettes clarons ranne vpon sarazyns couragyously whiche stalked agaynste grete pryde daye acquytayne moche pyteous batayll dyed valyaunt knyghtes men eche estate many bloode ranne felde lyke lytell ryuer gyaunt ferragus entred ye batayll also nere neue dromadyan bare bancre myght aboute hym grete puyssaunce sarazyns defende smote vpon christen men impetuously houre slewe syxe valyaunt knyghtes wyte b • udumayn bondry wyllyam galeram anthony good marshall hardy gloryam whiche next good duke acquytain christen men asprely assaylled cursed sarazyns constrained recole abacke good duke acquytayne enclosed enemyes abode alone without ony helpe socoure whiche dide suche feates armes none durste abyde hī cryed acquytayne agaynste cursed false sarazyns nothynge auaylled prowesse also • e kynge ferragus aspyed hym knewe hym wente towarde toke ledde awaye whan bounde hym surely made hym ledde pauylyon whiche moche ryche pleasaunt ferragus retorned batayll vpon christian iournay euyl christen men losse theyr good maister wolde haue taken flight ualentine orson came cryinge righte hyghe ualyaunte knyghtes acquytayne shewe chyualry faylled nede shuld greate reproche haue hardy courage good heart god shal healpe thus recomforted two knightes people acquitaine fete hadde almoost fledde manner retorned vpon sarasins agayn began batayl stronger befoore tidinges befoore acquytayne duke taken prysoner bothe litel great wepte takynge aboue dolorus incomparable piteous complaynt fayre fezonne wryngyng handes pullynge heer bryghter thā golde wyre saying syghinge hearte wepynge tenderly eyen ala poore sorowful happened thou art moste vnfortuned vpon erth alasse dere fader nowe muste dye handes false sarazyns neuer departe escape bydde fare wel ryght swete fader shal neuer se shall abyde vnpu • uayed poore orphelin ferre plesaunce nere dyscomfort bytter dolorous ala orson good louer longe abyding ought well noye herte yf present ye wold deliuer father sorowfull ¶ maner weapte lamented fayre pleasaunt fezonne christen mē sarazius fought vpon feld much impetuously one another batayll endured longe wyth deed wyth wounded al earth couered noble valyaunte knyghte ualentyne sharp swerd made greate occysyon sarazyns ther none hardy durst byde orson side swore god saintes finish hys dayes batrayll wold go fetch duke acquytayne wythin tent gyaunt ferragus pacolet beside hym gaue good comfort promysed hym socour sweryng hys god would fayll hym hys nede orson smote hors sporres entred batayll soo fyersly euer sted brooke batayll passed whan orson pacolet passed batayll hurled theyr shieldes dobone hanged theyr neckes sarazyns sheldes wherin ymage mahoune paynted wente vnto pauylyon gyaunt ferragus without ony said contrari pacolet coude speke theyr language ryghte well entred tentes ha • e good duke whanne pacolet sawe manye sarazyns kept hym wente played wyth hys charmes well subtyllye made lye dawne slepe whan sleap • orson came vnto duke acquytayne sayd vn hym fre duke come mount vppon thys hors wythout ony taryinge handes ferragus shall delyuer • ou knight halle asked wage daye gaue ¶▪ pounde hauen • ere painims without dauger shall leade hoost knyghte sayd duke • e ryght welcome casteth oute seruage delyuereth mortall enemyes good hym dommage gyue doughter haue well wonne shall haue maryage halfe coūtre acquytayne gramercy sayd knyght suche gyfte refused thynke make dylygence escape place retorne vnto hoost thre champyons duke acquytayne orson pacolet toke armes sarazyns passed theyr waye without contradyccion ony body goo vnto christen hoost ¶ durynge tyme orson wente towarde duke acquitayne ualentyne batayll demaunded dyuers broder orson none coude tell tydynges knowledge hym wherfore ualentyne ryght sorowful angrye herte wende ben slayne batayll wherfore made many pyteous cryes saynge ala vsurped bytter fortune sydes ioyes well chaunged sorowe dystresse whan haue loste pryncipall frende floure comforte hope lyfe ala fayre broder orson haue loste false sarazyns knowe well youre valyauntes hardynes cause dethe shortynge knowe moche wyll ra ther dye valyauntly lyue reproche shame ala valyaunt broder orson payne trauayl conquered wodde syth haue kepte peryll daunger nowe whan purposed thought haue solace myrthe ye separed gone syth haue tydynges maner wyse swere promyse god shall knowe shortlye fynde quycke deed youre loue shal dethe anone dolorous wordes entred noble knyght valentyn batayll man dyscomforted charged wt melancoly helde swerde fyne stele hande shewed suche knyght hode body euer rested ony slewe syxe seuen paynyms deed erthe doynge prowesse gyaunte ferragus knewe wente warde broder retorne agayne haue doubte thanne ualentine retorned towarde hym whiche conquered hym ahors mounted vpon hym pacolet amongest hoost sarazyns cryed ryght hyghe portingale makynge crye passed batayl came vnto hoost christen men delyuered hādes theyr enemyes whan christen men sawe duke delyuered theyr courage grewe theyr force doubled joyous cryed one voyce lyue acquytayne makynge noyse sauary baron knyghtes whan duke acquytayne retorned palays sente lordes knyghtes con • te doughter ye fayre fezunne syth called orson asked name orson subtyll sayd syr called rycharde duke acquytayne sayd lordes knowe trouthe aboue thynges beholden wyll honoure done vnto knyght presence hym retorned acquytayne haue ben delyuered myn aduersary mortall enemye doughter wyll desyre haue maryage valyaunte knyghte aboue holde hym may holde hym moost valaunt excellente grete prowesse hathe shewed towerde haue promysed guerdond rewarde gentyll body lawe mariage shall wedded vnto well oughte ue hym whan hathe loued fader moche hathe saued lyfe ¶ oppynyon duke cōsentynge baron noble knyghtes courte sayd comyn accorde knyghte well worthy haue fayre lady mariage hadde done grete prowesse fade • sake orsō presence wolde declare vppon dead oppynyon vntyll ye tyme assayed courage wyll fayre fezonne euen enterprysed tolde broder ualentyne ¶ orson wolde assaye wyl loyalte fayre fezonne wedded capitulo xxxix orson wyse subtyl wedded fayre fezone wolde knowe assaye yf kepe fayth sted faste loyal oftentymes herde saye woman suche nature lytell thynge chaunged theyr thoughtes promyses broke theym falsly well dyuers ben suche nature yt vyces shrewed ought taken aleged corrumpe loyalte good one amongest abuswe thornes oftentymes founde florysshed rose also amonge grete sorte euyl woman maye well founden one good one happe euen fezonne whiche orson founde loyall sayd vnto duke maner assaye syr honoure bounden thāke regarde doughter wolde well knowe wyll apperteyneth well haue man hygher estate therfore take wyll speke knowe wyll courage maryage done agaynst wyll cometh lyghtly vnto perfeccyon knyghte sayd duke acquytayne haue good reason accorde go chaumbre speke ende better enfourmed case wordes entred chambre fayre fezonne sat hym downe besyde syth toke hande sayd vnto muche swetely lady grete beaute hathe taken sore loue withoute haue none alegemente nowe thanked god whan hathe pleased hym doo suche grace wyfe gyuen may well vaunte al haue fayrest loue syth pleaseth good duke fader haue husbande ye oughte well reason contente shall serue holde parfyte loyalte durynge tyme lyfe wherfore praye ryghte dere lady ye haue remembraunce one vpon ye wyll enbrace kysse presente tyne refuse louynge requeste praye syth tyme come muste assembled ought refuse wyll▪ knyght answered lady wel taught demaū suche thynges ought refrayne lese payne loue knyghtes men good dedes goodnes honoure aboue al loue one hym wil loue kepe faith loyalte haue sworne vnto hym neuer wil chaūge forget lady said orson ought reason please whan pleaseth father syr sayde mayden well reason obeye vnto lorde father happen constrayne vnto suche thyng would gyue vnto hym conquered grene knyght shall rather departe hym without beryng thyng saue fayth god lady sayd orson • u • yll muche sore • n amoured knyght knowe wylde nature cannot speake saye one worde wherby myght reioyce tell wil syr said lady true loue learneth loue naturally said comōly thing pleased one halfe solde wherfore fre knight haue trust neuer life wil • ha • ge hym haue promysed fayth orson muche ioyous wysdome fezonne gaue aunswere made semblaune ill contente departed chambre without takyng leue wente towarde duke sayde hym free duke knowe come speakyng doughter hath geuen • ynall aunswere neuer lyfe man speaketh wyl haue vnto husbād conquered grene knight knyght said duke aunswere care lyeth wyll lytell pacient ano • e nothynge daye shal speke doughter ferder mater gramercye sayd orson beholden vnto orson yssued palays went vnto lodging brother ualentyne whome tolde recounted answere bene gyuen hym fayre fezonne broder haue wrought well thys ought suffise may wel know great loyalte loue loueth wyl go toward palays togider also sone duke shal se certayne shall ryght well receyued syr sayd orson wyl bee done ualentyne arayed hym precyous clothes orson toke • ace • fyrst whan came perfyte secrete loue ryght well founden haue desyred muche haue abyden long tyme howe well syth tyme demaunded father hathe maryed notwithstandyng hath bene courage neuer hated man muche kyng lucar husbande nowe may well saye hath pleasure euer shall haue sythe god hath geuen grace haue founde requyre haue none nowe myne amerous accomplyshed entierly lady sayde kyng doubte shall neuer fayle swere thre dayes passed shall make quene ynde grete maistresse tenementes saying wordes kyng ynde rode leadyng awaye pleasaunt lady rozemonde gardes maydens pauylion great haste ranne vnto kyng lucar sayde hym syr euyll tydinges daye haue loste great losse kyng ynde enemy leadeth waye pleasaunt lady rozemonde vpon horse presently hath stolen taken awaye wherfore make men folowe hym saue lady honoure nowe holde peace sayd kyng lucar tell therof hath euyll wyfe leseth ought lytell sorowful thus aunswered kyng lucar full sory harte without cause wente towarde kynge brandyffer sayd hym maner speke ualentine left empire grece lāde • uerpe went constantinoble receiued orson muche honourably mornynge hugon called fayre clerymonde sayde fayre language lady knowe kyng hongrye holde vnder diuers▪ greace lordes one thyng euill haue wyfe • mary whiche thyng come ward haue vnderstande knyghte ualentyne wil neuer retourne wherfore require yt haue husbande shal crowned quene hongrye greately honoured aboue harte desyreth • dauntlye syr sayn lady good honour present thanke humbly aunswere well seke another wyfe loue ualentine lyueth yet soo delybreed abyde hym seuen yere whan delyuered go vnto rusalem sor vysyte holy sepulcre wold gladly wolde bere company syr sayde orson contente wyll go angorye take grene knyght v kyng therof pleaseth well sayd kyng hugon lette v go wyll mahowne sayd vnto kynge vnderstondome shall tell thynge prouffyte knowe syr newly aryued two knightes ought hate aboue al haue slayne kynge brandyffer kynge lucar puyssaunt kynge ynde brother whan rabastre vnderstode hys brother dead wepte much sayd vnto hugon syr yelde two knyghtes yes sayd traytour hugon yt wyll giue theyr seales af golde syr sayd kyng surye ingrate yf refused soo lytell thynge shall haue seales thynges ynoughe yf may delyuer two knyghtes yes sayd hugon herken sende messenger house patryarke tel kynge sury dyd sent viii hundred men armed good patryarke whyche shewed lodgys kynges cōmaundement paynyms went thyther anone founde orson grene knyght dynner▪ whyche tooke bounde straytely betynge theym ledde towarde kynge ala sayd orson betrayed ryght kynge pepyn twelue peres fraunce one solde vnto sarazyns thys cyte nowe whan kynge sury sawe sayd vnto false enemyes oure lawe ryght joyous holde tel name wyll knowe theym cause syr sayde orson called orson thys grene knyght mahowne sayd kynge haue hearde muche speke haue felowe named valentyne whiche helde shoulde neuer escape handes lyue made dyspoyled tooke theyr seales frome theym whyche gaue afterwarde kynge hugon orson grene knyght put depe dongeon bread water longe thought kyng hugon b • slayne sarazyns ala knew nothing mater go traytoure hugon cytye yt called vnto disloyall traytoure named bare heart ¶ whan bellyssant sawe clerymonde dis • omforted soo sayd vnto doughter take pa • yen • e knowe sonne ought sorowfull heart whan consider remedye better praye hys soule wepe muche thinke brother emperour orson maundeth ala sayd clerymonde wherof speke maryage maye make trusteth neuer haue joye lady god speake therof wyl neuer haue husbande doughter sayd bellyssant euyll auysed syth hyghe man kynge hugon wyll haue shall neuer praysed tell well maye suche one come ye shall mary wordes fayre clerimonde entred chambre sore wepynge valentyne vnder stayres thinketh hys heart whens suche treason may come happened ende foure dayes kynge hugon arryued constantynoble receyued grett honoure fayre clerymonde made hym semblaūt loue lady sayd haue wel heard sonne dead wherof sory accorded shall haue clerymonde vnto wyfe syr sayd clerymonde haue wyl wedde none ualentyne heard treason thynge soo moche pleded accorded laste haue kyng hugon wherof muche joyous dured longe ¶ bellyssant clerimonde knew treason false enterpryse kyng hugon prduost smote head galeran ca cxv ualentyne greate pite loue yt betraye entred chapel lady accustomed pray god kneled downe ymage vyrgyn thou sayest haue certayn tydinges dead lady sayd ualentyne ought beleue deliuer vnto death bee yet lyue thou shalt se within thre dayes▪ whā hugon herde wordes ualentyne tolde vnto ye ladyes yssued secretly palays mounted vpō horse without retourning lady muche amarueiled woulde haue feasted pylgrym would nothing said ladyes pardon haue felowes towne whiche wil go se clerimonde gaue much money orson joyous desyred muche hys comynge night orson laye galazye engendred sōne called morant whiche helde realme angorye longe orson reised hoost go angorye whan kynge hugon knewe sente messenger vnto hym sayenge wolde accorde wolde leue hym cyte angory▪ gyue hym foure horse laden wyth golde yf accused treason▪ wolde fyght wyth hym excepte orson message done grene knight waged batayll kinge hugon came angory armed fight wyth grene knight accorded grene knighte fyrst thā smote theyr horse spore recoū • ted eche broke theyr speres set theyr handes vnto theyr swerdes god wote stroke gaue eche muche god helped ryght grene knyght gaue suche stroke vnto kyng hugon vpon helme cut part head sholdres fell sooo • ne grene knyght honoured hugon spake demaunded confessoure tolde hym falsnes myserye wythout geuyng ony knowledge ala haue sene often pouertye▪ colde trauayle wythout geuyng comforte▪ nowe aboue moost vnfortuned whan might know aduyse ought serue longe bytter trybulacyon▪ true angory ¶ merueylous vysion orson hebe • heremyte great wodde ca cxv • mithin seuen yere galazyedyed emperour orson made great sorow deeth ete brede rote small froytes founde wodde dyd remayne happened hym one nyght vysyon hym semed sawe gate heuen open sawe joyes saued syeges sayntes crowned glorye aungelles songe melodyously sauyour world sawe betwene two hyghe roches botom obscure valeye gulfre helle dampned brennynge fyre boylynge caudrous hanged theyr tongue assaylled enuyronned wyth serpentes generally sawe paynes helle whiche horrible ferefull recounte whyche vysyon wakened afrayed ameruaylled thynges sene wepyng pyteously came vnto grene knyght sayd hym frende knowe worlde lytell valoure shorte durynge vayne glorye pompes worlde displeasaunt vnto god salute soule lytle profytable whyche thynge praye wyll take kepe vpon chyldren enfourme dedes condycyons maye gouerne empyre grece pleasure god worlde leue charge vnto hym aboue men world trust mooste knowe remnaunte lyfe wyll lede solytaryly habandone worlde houre renoū ce worldly honoure take leue yf whan grene knyght heard wrodes beganne wepe tenderly orson recomforted hym sayd ala wepe praye vnto god giue strengthe puyssaunce accomplysshe wyll orson departed defendynge grene knyghte tell anye body wente greate wodde lyued holyly deathe god shewed many myracles saynt canonyzed grene knyght gouerned chyldren finisshed dayes gloriouslye wente vnto blysse neuer shall haue ende bryng v suffered deathe v crosse amen ¶ thus endeth hystorye two valyaunte brother ualentine orson sōnes vnto emperour
